##德国专员辖区决议##
#Category only allowed for GER
GER_reichskommissariats = {
	波希米亚和摩拉维亚帝国保护领 = {
		icon = ger_reichskommissariats
		available = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_form_the_reichskommissariats
			has_government = fascism
			9 = {
				is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_puppet = yes
			}
			75 = {
				is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_puppet = yes
			}
		}
		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = yes
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000 modifier = { factor = 0 has_war_with_major = yes }
		}
		visible = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_form_the_reichskommissariats
			has_government = fascism
		}
		complete_effect = { hidden_effect = { every_subject_country = { inherit_technology = GER } }#guo
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 9
							state = 75
						}
						is_owned_by = GER
					}
				}
				9 = {
					add_core_of = R01
				}
				75 = {
					add_core_of = R01
				}
			}
			R01 = {
				set_state_controller = 9
				set_state_owner = 9
				set_state_controller = 75
				set_state_owner = 75
				GER = {
					puppet = PREV hidden_effect = { every_subject_country = { inherit_technology = GER } }#guo
					if = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								has_dlc = "Death or Dishonor"
							}
						}
						set_autonomy = {
							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
							end_wars = no
						}
					}
					else = {
						set_autonomy = {
							target = PREV
							autonomy_state = autonomy_reichskommissariat
							end_wars = no
						}
					}
				}
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "德意志临时总督"
					desc = "POLITICS_ARTHUR_SEYSS_INQUART_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/GER/Portrait_Germany_Military_Administration.dds"
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = nazism
					traits = { prince_of_terror#guo
					}
				}
				set_capital = {
					state = 9
					remember_old_capital = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
